    </span></span></div></div></div><strong><span>Returned within the following response objects:</span></strong><ul class="list list--disc list"><li><code class="syntax-inline requests:</span></strong></p><div><h5>Attributes</h5><div class="api-table"><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="additional_processor_response"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#additional_processor_response" ariel-label="additional_processor_response">additional_processor_response</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Optional additional processor response information, provided as further context for the primary <a href="#processor_response_code">processor response</a>.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="amount"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#amount" ariel-label="amount">amount</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">BigDecimal</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The amount used when verifying the card.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_error_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_error_response_code" ariel-label="avs_error_response_code">avs_error_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">This field is populated if there was an error when checking AVS or the processing bank does not support AVS. Possible values:</p>
<ul class=" list list--disc">
<li><code>S</code> = Issuing bank does not support AVS</li>
<li><code>E</code> = AVS system error</li>
</ul>
<br/>
<p class=" markdown-p">If this value is <!-- -->nil<!-- -->, you will see responses in both <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby#avs_postal_code_response_code">avs_postal_code_response_code</a></code> and <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby#avs_street_address_response_code">avs_street_address_response_code</a></code>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_postal_code_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_postal_code_response_code" ariel-label="avs_postal_code_response_code">avs_postal_code_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>This is populated if the processor supports the address verification system (AVS). Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>M</code> = Matches</li><li><code>N</code> = Does not match</li><li><code>U</code> = Not verified</li><li><code>I</code> = Not provided</li><li><code>A</code> = Not applicable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="avs_street_address_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#avs_street_address_response_code" ariel-label="avs_street_address_response_code">avs_street_address_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>This is populated if the processor supports the address verification system (AVS). Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>M</code> = Matches</li><li><code>N</code> = Does not match</li><li><code>U</code> = Not verified</li><li><code>I</code> = Not provided</li><li><code>A</code> = Not applicable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="billing"><div class="api-field"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Country code of phone number. 1-3 digits. Required.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-2 type-string api-table-row " id="national_number"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#national_number" ariel-label="national_number">national_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>National number of phone number. 4-12 digits. Required.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="last_name"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#last_name" ariel-label="last_name">last_name</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The last name.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="locality"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#locality" ariel-label="locality">locality</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The locality/city.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="phone_number"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#phone_number" ariel-label="phone_number">phone_number</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p><strong>Deprecated.</strong></p><p><em>We recommend using <code>international_phone</code>. </p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="token"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#token" ariel-label="token">token</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The Vault token for the credit card.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="unique_number_identifier"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#unique_number_identifier" ariel-label="unique_number_identifier">unique_number_identifier</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>A randomly-generated string that uniquely identifies a credit card number in the Vault. If the same credit card is added to a merchant&#x27;s Vault multiple times, each Vault entry will have the same unique identifier. This value is randomly generated by merchant gateway account, so it will be different for each merchant&#x27;s Vault.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="currency_iso_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#currency_iso_code" ariel-label="currency_iso_code">currency_iso_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The currency of the verification amount (e.g. &quot;USD&quot; for US dollars). See the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_4217">ISO 4217</a> codes.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="cvv_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#cvv_response_code" ariel-label="cvv_response_code">cvv_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>The processing bank&#x27;s response to the card verification value (CVV) provided by the customer. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>M</code> = Matches</li><li><code>N</code> = Does not match</li><li><code>U</code> = Not verified</li><li><code>I</code> = Not provided</li><li><code>S</code> = Issuer does not participate</li><li><code>A</code> = Not applicable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="gateway_rejection_reason"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#gateway_rejection_reason" ariel-label="gateway_rejection_reason">gateway_rejection_reason</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name"></span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">This value will only be set if the transaction status is <span class="formatConstant">gateway_rejected</span>. Possible values:</p>
<ul class=" list list--disc">
<li><code>&quot;application_incomplete&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;avs&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;avs_and_cvv&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;cvv&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;duplicate&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;fraud&quot;</code></li>
<li><code>&quot;three_d_secure&quot;</code></li>
</ul></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="graphql_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#graphql_id" ariel-label="graphql_id">graphql_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The unique identifier used to identify this credit card verification in Braintree&#x27;s GraphQL API.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#id" ariel-label="id">id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The string value representing a specific credit card verification in the Vault. <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/best-practices#token-and-id-lengths-and-formats">Length and format of gateway-generated tokens and IDs may change at any time</a>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="merchant_account_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#merchant_account_id" ariel-label="merchant_account_id">merchant_account_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The <a href="/braintree/articles/control-panel/important-gateway-credentials#merchant-account-id">merchant account ID</a> used for the credit card verification. Currency is also determined by merchant account ID.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="network_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#network_response_code" ariel-label="network_response_code">network_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">The network response code. When present, this field can provide additional detail about why a verification was declined, but the <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby#processor_response_code">processor_response_code</a></code> should be considered the source of truth. See the list of <a data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;link_to_example_com&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;navigate to example.com&quot;}" href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#network-response-codes">possible network responses</a>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="network_response_text"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#network_response_text" ariel-label="network_response_text">network_response_text</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">The network response text for the <code class="syntax-inline syntax-inline--theme"><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby#network_response_code">network_response_code</a></code>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="processor_response_code"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#processor_response_code" ariel-label="processor_response_code">processor_response_code</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The processor response code. See the list of <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses">possible processor authorization responses</a>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="processor_response_text"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#processor_response_text" ariel-label="processor_response_text">processor_response_text</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The processor response text. See the list of <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses">possible processor authorization responses</a>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="processor_response_type"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#processor_response_type" ariel-label="processor_response_type">processor_response_type</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>The processor response type. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>&quot;approved&quot;</code></li><li><code>&quot;soft_declined&quot;</code></li><li><code>&quot;hard_declined&quot;</code></li></ul><p>See the list of <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses">possible processor authorization responses</a>, and definitions of <a href="/braintree/docs/reference/general/processor-responses/authorization-responses#types-of-declines">soft and hard declines</a>.</p></div></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="risk_data"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#risk_data" ariel-label="risk_data">risk_data</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">map</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Any applicable risk data associated with the verification. The data includes the risk identifier, the device data captured flag, and the risk decision, which can provide further context on how a transaction was scored by Braintree.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="decision"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#decision" ariel-label="decision">decision</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>The risk decision. Possible values:</p><ul><li>Not Evaluated</li><li>Approve</li><li>Review</li><li>Decline</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="decision_reasons"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#decision_reasons" ariel-label="decision_reasons">decision_reasons</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">map</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>An array of strings containing the rules triggered by the fraud provider when generating the decision.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="device_data_captured"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#device_data_captured" ariel-label="device_data_captured">device_data_captured</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Flag indicating whether device session data was successfully captured and processed by the fraud service.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="fraud_service_provider"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#fraud_service_provider" ariel-label="fraud_service_provider">fraud_service_provider</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The fraud service used to determine if a transaction is likely to be fraudulent.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#id" ariel-label="id">id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The risk data identifier.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="transaction_risk_score"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#transaction_risk_score" ariel-label="transaction_risk_score">transaction_risk_score</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The score returned by the fraud provider as a measurement of the transaction&#x27;s likelihood for being fraudulent.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="status"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#status" ariel-label="status">status</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p class=" markdown-p">Possible values:</p>
<ul class=" list list--disc">
<li>
<span class="formatConstant">processor_declined</span>
</li>
<li>
<span class="formatConstant">gateway_rejected</span>
</li>
<li>
<span class="formatConstant">failed</span>
</li>
<li>
<span class="formatConstant">verified</span>
</li>
</ul></p></span></div></div><div class="type-string api-table-row grand-master-parent" id="three_d_secure_info"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_info" ariel-label="three_d_secure_info">three_d_secure_info</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">obj</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/3d-secure/overview">3D Secure</a> information for this transaction.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="cavv"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#cavv" ariel-label="cavv">cavv</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Cardholder Authentication Verification Value or &quot;CAVV&quot;. The main encrypted message issuers and card networks use to verify authentication has occured. Mastercard refers to this field as AAV, while American Express refers to this field as AEVV.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="ds_transaction_id"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#ds_transaction_id" ariel-label="ds_transaction_id">ds_transaction_id</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Transaction identifier resulting from 3D Secure 2 authentication.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="eci_flag"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#eci_flag" ariel-label="eci_flag">eci_flag</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>The value of the electronic commerce indicator (ECI) flag, which indicates the outcome of the 3DS authentication.</p><p>Possible values for Mastercard:</p><ul><li><code>00</code> = Failed or not attempted</li><li><code>01</code> = Attempted</li><li><code>02</code> = Success</li><li><code>04</code> = Data-Only (Applies to limited processors)</li></ul><p>Possible values for all other card brands:</p><ul><li><code>07</code> = Failed or not attempted</li><li><code>06</code> = Attempted</li><li><code>05</code> = Success</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="enrolled"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#enrolled" ariel-label="enrolled">enrolled</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><div><p>Indicates whether a card is enrolled in a 3D Secure program or not. Possible values:</p><ul><li><code>Y</code> = Yes</li><li><code>N</code> = No</li><li><code>U</code> = Unavailable</li><li><code>B</code> = Bypass</li><li><code>E</code> = RequestFailure</li></ul></div></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="liability_shift_possible"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#liability_shift_possible" ariel-label="liability_shift_possible?">liability_shift_possible?</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Indicates whether a liability shift is possible.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="liability_shifted"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#liability_shifted" ariel-label="liability_shifted?">liability_shifted?</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">bool</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Indicates whether the liability shifted or not.</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="status"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#status" ariel-label="status">status</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><p>The 3D Secure status value. For a list of all possible statuses and their liability shifts, see the <a href="/braintree/docs/guides/3d-secure/server-side#status-codes">3D Secure guide</a>.</p></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="three_d_secure_version"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#three_d_secure_version" ariel-label="three_d_secure_version">three_d_secure_version</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>The version of 3D Secure authentication used for the transaction. Composed of digits separated by periods (e.g. <code>1.0.2</code>, <code>2.1.0</code>).</span></p></span></div></div><div class="indent-1 type-string api-table-row " id="xid"><div class="api-field"><span class="hash-link-container"><code><a href="#xid" ariel-label="xid">xid</a></code></span><span class="type"><span class="type__name">String</span></span></div><div class="api-definition"><span class="description"><p class="markdown-p"><span>Transaction identifier resulting from 3D Secure authentication. This field will no longer be used in 3D Secure 2 authentications.</span></p></span></div></div></div></div><h2 id="product-id-codes" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Product ID codes</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#product-id-codes" aria-label="Product ID codes"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>The Braintree gateway returns the following product IDs for credit and debit card payment methods.

</div><h2 id="network-response-codes" class="test_h2 markdown-h2"><span>Network response codes</span><a class="icon icon--link hash-link" href="#network-response-codes" aria-label="Network response codes"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/btdevdoc/bundles/4.3.24/_assets/anchor-PKYVW2VT.svg" alt="AnchorIcon"/></a></h2><p class="markdown-p"><span>In addition to the </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#processor_response_code"><span>processor response code</span></a><span> and text, some transaction
        and verification objects also include a </span><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#network_response_code"><span>network response code</span></a><span> and text.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>These network response values are the raw responses that may be returned by the card network, and
        when present they can provide additional detail about why a request was approved or declined.
        However, this information is supplemental to the processor response code; you should consider the
        processor response code to be the source of truth.</span></p><p class="markdown-p"><span>Each card network has distinct response codes:</span></p><ul class="list list--disc"><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#card-network-visa"><span>Visa</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#card-network-mastercard"><span>Mastercard</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#card-network-discover"><span>Discover</span></a></li><li><a href="/braintree/docs/reference/response/credit-card-verification/ruby/#card-network-american-express"><span>American Express</span></a></li></ul><div class="ppvx_table ecmTable docsTable"><table>
<thead>

over","","","","","","","","","|","65","","","|","Exceeds","withdrawal","count","limit","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","|\n|","Discover","","","","","","","","","|","66","","","|","Card","Acceptor","call","Acquirers","security","dept","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","","" object**](/braintree/docs/reference/general/result-objects)  **from the following requests:**\n\n\n## Product ID codes\n\nThe Braintree gateway returns the following product IDs for credit and debit card payment methods. The product ID is generally 1-3 characters and indicates the specific credit product that was issued to the customer.\n\n\n\n## Network response codes\n\nIn addition to the [processor response code](#processor_response_code) and text, some transaction and verification objects also include a [network response code](#network_response_code) and text.\n\nThese network response values are the raw responses that may be returned by the card network, and when present they can provide additional detail about why a request was approved or declined.
